Search within

Search within the title, abstract, claims, or full patent document: You can restrict your search to a specific field using field names.

Use TI= to search in the title, AB= for the abstract, CL= for the claims, or TAC= for all three. For example, TI=(safety belt).

Search by Cooperative Patent Classifications (CPCs): These are commonly used to represent ideas in place of keywords, and can also be entered in a search term box. If you're searching forseat belts, you could also search for B60R22/00 to retrieve documents that mention safety belts or body harnesses. CPC=B60R22 will match documents with exactly this CPC, CPC=B60R22/low matches documents with this CPC or a child classification of this CPC.

Find patents

Keywords and boolean syntax (USPTO or EPO format): seat belt searches these two words, or their plurals and close synonyms. "seat belt" searches this exact phrase, in order. -seat -belt searches for documents not containing either word.

For searches using boolean logic, the default operator is AND with left associativity. Note: this means safety OR seat belt is searched as (safety OR seat) AND belt. Each word automatically includes plurals and close synonyms. Adjacent words that are implicitly ANDed together, such as (safety belt), are treated as a phrase when generating synonyms.

Learn More
Search by

Chemistry searches match terms (trade names, IUPAC names, etc. extracted from the entire document, and processed from .MOL files.)

Substructure (use SSS=) and similarity (use ~) searches are limited to one per search at the top-level AND condition. Exact searches can be used multiple times throughout the search query.

Searching by SMILES or InChi key requires no special syntax. To search by SMARTS, use SMARTS=.

To search for multiple molecules, select "Batch" in the "Type" menu. Enter multiple molecules separated by whitespace or by comma.

It can also be used to treat local infections caused by a variety of Candida, Trichoderma, Microsporum or Epidermophilia (such as Trichomonas esculenta, Crimson red bacteria, Microsporum canis or Trichophyton floccus), or caused by Mucosal infection caused by Candida albicans. ___ -14- This paper uses the Chinese National Standard (CNS) A4 ^ (210X297mm) (Please read the precautions on the back before filling this page)

Description of the invention (12) The compound of formula (I) can also be used for the treatment of various filamentous mycetes such as Geotrichum clavatum, Mycelia ( Such as B. gerbilii), Blastoschizomyces (such as BlastozochimyCes capitatus), spore mycelia (such as S. sclerotiorum) Scedosporium (such as Scedosporium apiosperum), Cladosporium (such as Scavenger spores) Infections caused by bottle-shaped yeast. The in vitro evaluation of the anti-smear activity of the compounds of the present invention is performed on liquid or solid media using a two-fold serial dilution technique of anti-smear bacteria. This technique measures the inhibition of anti-smear agents at 37 C after 24 to 48 hours The minimum inhibitory concentration (MIC) of the growth of Candida. In practice, clinically relevant pathogens, such as Candida albicans, are cultivated with a series of agar plates or broth microdilution series containing a double dilution of antimycobacterial agent. Then measure the growth of the candida in the agar dish or broth microdilution series and record the appropriate MI C value. The MF C value (that is, the minimum concentration of anti-mycobacteria that kills at least 99.9% of pathogens in the original liquid medium) will be determined by subculture of 0.01 and 0.1 microliter broth in the control cavity without drug. Pathogens grow in the recesses, and other soil fat dish recesses grow without pathogens. The in vivo evaluation of the compound of formula (I) is based on a series of different dosimetry in which administration (eg, subcutaneous administration, oral administration, intraperitoneal administration or intravenous administration) is inoculated with Candida albicans strains. Untreated mice died within 3 to 9 days, and the dose that prevented 50% of infected mice from dying was recorded. -15- Use the Chinese National Standard Rate (CNS) 84 specifications (21x297mm) (please read the precautions on the back before filling out this page). . 1T. The compound of formula (i) has antimycobacterial activity and can be used to treat various infections of human mycetes. Such infections include surface, skin, subcutaneous, and systemic fungal infections, such as respiratory infections, gastrointestinal infections, cardiovascular infections, urinary tract infections, central nervous system (CNS) infections, candidiasis, and candidal candidiasis Diseases (such as thrush and vaginal candidiasis) and skin infections caused by candidiasis, candidiasis of the skin and mucous membranes, skin candidiasis including addiction and white addiction infections, Hong Kong foot, paronychia, variegation Ringworm, red addiction, abrasion, mycobacterial alveolar'candidiasis vulvitis and otitis externa. Pharmaceutically acceptable salts can also be prepared from other salts, including other pharmaceutically acceptable salts of compounds of formula (1), using conventional methods. Metabolically unstable esters of compounds of formula (I) can be prepared by reaction with the existing bases by conventional methods. Similarly, metabolically unstable esters can also be formed with free radicals present on the molecule. The novel compound of formula (XII) can be prepared according to the fermentation method described later, or can be prepared by demethylation of sodarin by a biotransformation method. The fermentation method involves culturing a microorganism capable of producing the compound of formula (XII), and then separating the compound of formula (XII) from the culture. The microorganism capable of producing the compound of formula (XII) may be a variant of D. arachnoides. This strain can be confirmed by analyzing the survival rate of the mutant by screening test samples obtained by fermentation of microorganisms by standard methods. In particular, the microorganisms that are convenient to use are the strains of arachnid coccidioides stored in the constant culture collection of CAB International Mycological Institute, Genetic Resource Reference Collection Bakeham Lane, Egham, Surrey TW20 9TY, United Kingdom. This strain was received by this organization on June 10, 1994, and the acquisition number was given as IMI 362184, and the date of receipt and the date of confirmation of survival were indicated on June 13, 1994 and 21, respectively. This institution is accepted as an international depository (Internatinai Depository) authority under the Buda Pace Treaty. For the characteristics proven so far by IMI 362 184, see Example 74. These methods include ionizing radiation, chemical methods such as N-methyl-N'-nitro-N-nitroisomai (n TG), thermal 'gene technology' such as gene recombination and gene conversion, treatment, and Selective natural variant technology. The preparation of the compound of formula (XII) by fermentation can be accomplished by traditional methods, that is, cultivating suitable microorganisms in the presence of assimilable sources of carbon, nitrogen, and mineral salts, and then isolating the desired product. The sources of assimilable carbon, nitrogen, and mineral salts can be supplied by simple or compound nutrients. Carbon sources generally include glucose, maltose, starch, glycerin, molasses dextrin, lactose, sucrose, fruit sugar, galactose, inositol, D_mannose 'soybean oil' carboxylic acid, amino acid 'glyceride, alcohol , Alkanes and vegetable oils. The carbon source generally constitutes 0.5 to 10% by weight of the fermentation base. Fruit sugar 'glucose and sucrose represent preferred carbon sources. Nitrogen sources generally include soybean meal, corn broth, lees, yeast extract, cottonseed meal, glands, ground hard fruit powder, malt extract, molasses, casein 'amino acid mixture, ammonia (gas or solution ), Ammonium or nitrate, urea and other amides can also be used. Nitrogen sources generally constitute 0.01 to 10% by weight of the fermentation base. The nutrient mineral salts that can be used in the culture medium include commonly used sodium, sodium, aluminum, iron, iron, zinc, aluminum, aluminum, phosphate, sulfate, Salts of vapors and carbonate ions. -40- This paper scale is applicable to China s B Family Standard (CNS) A4 specification (210X297 public daughter (please read the precautions on the back and then fill out this page) . Description of the invention (38) One *-The cultivation of microorganisms is generally at 20. To 40 C, preferably 2 . (: To 35C 'especially about 25. At the beginning of the medium can be inoculated with a small amount of mycelium and / or spores obtained The plant-based inoculum can be transferred to the fermentation substrate, or to one or more seed stages, where it is further grown, and then transferred to the main fermentation substrate. The fermentation is generally carried out at pH 3.5 to 9.5, preferably 4.5 to 7.5. It may be necessary to add alkali or acid to the fermentation substrate to maintain the pH in the desired range. Suitable alkalis that can be added include alkali metal hydroxides, such as aqueous sodium hydroxide or potassium hydroxide. Suitable acids include Mineral acids, such as hydrochloric acid, sulfuric acid or succinic acid .. Fermentation can be carried out 4-30 , Preferably about 5-15 days. To control excessive foaming, anti-foaming agent can be added, the time of addition depends on the need. Carbon and / or nitrogen source can also be added to the fermentation matrix as needed. Compound of formula (XII) Mainly attached to cells, it can be added with acid or water-soluble organic solvent, more preferably with alkali (such as sodium hydroxide) to make a solution. The cells in the solution can be separated by centrifugation, traditional filtration method or membrane filtration This liquid can be re-used with acid, such as sulfuric acid, if necessary, and treated to a pH of less than 6 (eg, about 4.5). The compound of formula (XII) can be separated and purified by various distribution techniques, such as washing away by adsorption, Shen Dian, classification: Crystallization, solvent extraction, and liquid-liquid distribution methods can also be used in combination. Separation and purification of the compound of formula (IX) is most suitable for adsorption on a solid support followed by washing away. Example 7 6 NCIMB 40675 NCIMB 40675 is aerobic 'Gram-positive, immobile irregular rods' in 28 C in 2% (weight / volume) yeast trypsin soybean At 48 hours of agar, lemon yellow, translucent, round, complete, raised, 0.5 mm in diameter colonies were produced. This microorganism grows well up to 37C, but it does not grow better than this strain at 45 C. There are no metachromatic particles, but it is catalase-positive, oxidative, and cannot metabolize glucose by fermentation. This strain can use the following carbon sources: _D_glucose, D_fruit sugar, p-hydroxyphenylacetic acid, D_mannose, methyl \ pyruvate, lactamide, D-trehalose and sucrose . This microorganism can only use a little D-gluconate, pyruvate, and salicin as the main carbon source. The colony and microscope morphology are similar to Corynebacterium ^ The difference with Corynebacterium is that the peptidoglycan of NCIMB 40675 contains ornithine instead of 2,6 diaminopimelic acid or -216- This paper size is applicable Chinese National Standard (CNS) A4 ^ grid (2I0X297mm) (Please read the precautions on the back before filling in this page), - 321644 A7 B7 V. Description of the invention (214) The racemic difference of monoaminobutyric acid Structure. Moreover, this microbial-containing complex mixture of fat and acid is also different from that contained in coryneform bacteria, namely 12-methyltetradecanoic acid, 14-methylhexadecanoic acid and 14-methylpentadecanoic acid. No alpha-branched-A-hydroxylated fatty acids were also detected. Based on these results, ncimb 40675 is closest to the following species of Actinomyces: Aureobacillus, Curtobacterium, or Cellulomonas. To clarify the taxonomic position of NCIMB 40675, the 1100 base pair portion of the 16S rRNA gene is compared with 24 other species representing Actinobacteria and related genera. The results of this analysis show that NCIMB 40675 is more closely related to the genus Staphylococcus aureus and Curtobacterium, but farther away from the genus Cellulomonas and the genus Corynebacterium. For more accurate confirmation of this strain, in addition to more chemical taxonomy and physiology tests, phylogenetic analysis can be performed to compare the rRNA genes of various regions of Chrysanthemum aureus and Curtobacterium.
